fishki.adv.afterAdblockCheck = function(){

    function cookieOpt(expires)
    {
        return {
            expires: expires,
            path: '/',
            domain: 'fishki.net'
        };
    }

    function isCookieEnabled()
    {
        if ('cookie' in document &&
            (document.cookie = '__tst__=tst').indexOf.call(document.cookie, '__tst__') > -1) {
            document.cookie = '__tst__=; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 GMT';
            return true;
        }
        return false;
    }

    var ADB_COOKIE_DETECT = 'avoid';
    var ADB_COOKIE_USER = 'adb_uid';
    var ADB_COOKIE_USER_ID = 'Ajk4alug5j4qy0it9veuy';
    var ADB_COOKIE_MATCHING_SUCCESS = 'cmatched';

	if (!('showinlimbo' in window))
	{
        if (isCookieEnabled())
        {
            // Ставим куку детекта
            $.cookie(ADB_COOKIE_DETECT, 'yes', cookieOpt(1/8));
            // Если нет куки об успешном матчинге
            if (!$.cookie(ADB_COOKIE_MATCHING_SUCCESS))
            {
                $.cookie(ADB_COOKIE_USER, ADB_COOKIE_USER_ID, cookieOpt(30));
                $.cookie(ADB_COOKIE_MATCHING_SUCCESS, 'yes', cookieOpt(6));
                window.location = "https://an.yandex.ru/mapuid/fishkinet/Ajk4alug5j4qy0it9veuy?jsredir=1&sign=2290483577&location=http%3A%2F%2Ffishki.net%2Fgif%2F";
            }
        }
	}
	else
	{
        $.cookie(ADB_COOKIE_DETECT, '', cookieOpt(-1));
	}

	var test = document.createElement('div');
	test.innerHTML = ' ';
	test.className = 'adsbox';
	document.body.insertBefore(test, document.body.lastChild);
	document.body.appendChild(test);
	setTimeout(function(){

			document.body.classList.add('_ad-blocked');
		}
		else
        {
			fishki.is_adblock = false;
            window.showinlimbo = true;

        if (fishki && fishki.adv && fishki.adv.afterAdblockCheck)
            fishki.adv.afterAdblockCheck();

fishki.sliders = (function() {

    function init_ticker($s) {
        tm_start('init_ticker');
        var length = $s.find('.slide__item').length, mod = length % 5;
        if (mod)
            $('#the-ticker .slide__item:gt('+(length - mod-1)+')').remove();
        var parent_sizes = {};
        $(window).on('resize.the-ticker', function(){
            var $parent = null, resized = 0, $ticker = $('#the-ticker');
            tm_start('the-ticker inner resize');

            $ticker.find('.slide__item.meta_image img, .slide__item.scale_image img').each(function(){
                if (!$parent)
                    $parent = $(this).parents('.slide__item');
                if (!parent_sizes)
                {
                    parent_sizes.width = $parent.width();
                    parent_sizes.height = $parent.height();
                }
                if (parent_sizes.width == $parent.width())
                    return;
                resized++;
                fishki.utils.resizeMeCenter(this, $parent.width(), $parent.height());
            });
            if (!resized)
                $(window).off('resize.the-ticker');
            tm_end('the-ticker inner resize');
        });
        $(window).trigger('resize.the-ticker');
        tm_end('init_ticker');
    }


	function slider_init()
	{
        tm_start('slider_init');
		var $slider = $($.fn.cycle.defaults.autoSelector+':not(.inited)');
        $slider.each(function() {
            var $s = $(this);
            $s.addClass('inited');

            if (('showinlimbo' in window) && $s.find('.showlimbo_i').length)
                $s.find('.showlimbo_i').remove();
            if ($s.attr('id') === 'the-ticker')
                init_ticker($s);
            $s.on('cycle-prev cycle-next', function( event, opts ) {
                loadImages($s);
            });
            tm_start('$s.cycle');
            $s.cycle();
            tm_end('$s.cycle');
            $s.swipe();
        });

        $(function(){
            setTimeout(function() {
                $slider.each(function() {
                    loadImages($(this));
                });
            }, 1000)
        });

        $('img.lazy_load_image_past').each(function() {
			$(this).attr('src', $(this).data('src')).removeClass('lazy_load_image_past');
		});

        tm_end('slider_init');
	}

	function loadImages($slider)
	{
		if ($slider.find('img.lazy_load_image').length + $slider.find('a.lazy_load_image').length)
		{
			$slider.find('a.lazy_load_image').each(function(){
				var _this = this;
				$(_this).css('background-image', 'url(' + $(_this).data('src') + ')').ready(function() {
					$(_this).removeClass('lazy_load_image');
				});
			});

			$slider.find('img.lazy_load_image').each(function(){
				var _this = this;
				$(_this).attr('src', $(_this).data('src')).on('load', function() {
					$(_this).removeClass('lazy_load_image');
				});
			});
		}
	}

    function initthisslider(_this)
    {
        _this.removeClass('initthisslider');
        _this.find('.slider__arrow').unbind( "click" );
        var act = _this.find('.slider__arrow').data('action');
        var id = _this.find('.slider__arrow').data('id');
        _this.addClass('progress_slider_form');
        _this.find('.moderation').hide();
        _this.find('.progress_comment_img').show();
        $.ajax({
            type: 'post',
            data: 'action=' + act + '&id=' + id,
            url: '/getsimilar/',
            dataType: 'json',
            success: function(response) {
                if (response.hasOwnProperty('ok') && response.ok > 1) {
                    if (response.ok > 1) {
                        var hg = _this.height();
                        var wd = _this.width();
                        _this.parent().find('.toggles-wrap').remove();
                        _this.css('height', hg);
                        _this.css('overflow', 'hidden');
                        _this.find('.slide__item:last').after(response.html);
                        _this.attr('data-textid', 'textid_0');
                        _this.parent().find('.content__text:last').addClass('textid_0');
                        _this.parent().find('.content__text:last').after(response.html2);
                        _this.parent().find('.content__text:first').addClass('textid_0');
                        _this.parent().find('.content__text:first').after(response.html3);
                        _this.attr('data-cycle-fx', 'scrollHorz');
                        _this.attr('data-cycle-speed', 1000);
                        _this.attr('data-cycle-paused', true);
                        _this.attr('data-cycle-log', false);
                        _this.attr('data-cycle-slides', '.slide__item');
                        _this.attr('data-cycle-next', '>.slider__arrow--left');
                        _this.attr('data-cycle-prev', '>.slider__arrow--right');
                        var ln = (act=='next'?(_this.find('.slide__item').length-1):1);
                        _this.attr('data-starting-slide', ln);
                        _this.addClass('cycle-slideshow');
                        _this.parent().find('.content__text').addClass('hidden');
                        _this.parent().find('.textid_' + ln).removeClass('hidden');
                        _this.on( 'cycle-after', function(e, optionHash ) {
                            var sid = _this.find('.cycle-slide-active').data('textid');
                            _this.parent().find('.content__text').addClass('hidden');
                            _this.parent().find('.' + sid).removeClass('hidden');
                        });
                        var all = _this.find('.lazy_load_img img').length;
                        if (all > 0) {
                            _this.find('.lazy_load_img img').on('load', function() {
                                all--;
                                if (all == 0) {
                                    all--; // block
                                    _this.find('.lazy_load_img .post-img a>img').each(function() {
                                        var th = $(this);
                                        th.parent().parent().css('height', hg);
                                        var hg1 = th.height();
                                        var wd1 = th.width();
                                        if (wd1/hg1 > wd/hg) {
                                            th.css('height', hg);
                                            var wd2 = Math.floor(hg / hg1 * wd1) + 'px';
                                            var wd3 = '-' + Math.floor(hg / hg1 * wd1 / 2) + 'px';
                                            th.css('width', wd2);
                                            th.css('max-width', wd2);
                                            th.css('left', '50%');
                                            th.css('margin-left', wd3);
                                            th.css('position', 'absolute');
                                        } else {
                                            th.css('width', wd);
                                            var hd2 = Math.floor(wd / wd1 * hg1) + 'px';
                                            var hd3 = '-' + Math.floor(wd / wd1 * hg1 / 2) + 'px';
                                            th.css('height', hd2);
                                            th.css('max-height', hd2);
                                            th.css('top', '50%');
                                            th.css('margin-top', hd3);
                                            th.css('position', 'absolute');
                                        }
                                    });
                                    _this.find('.lazy_load_img').removeClass('lazy_load_img');
                                    _this.removeClass('progress_slider_form');
                                    _this.find('.progress_comment_img').hide();
                                    _this.cycle();
                                }
                            });
                        } else {
                            _this.cycle();
                        }
                    }
                } else {
                    _this.removeClass('progress_slider_form');
                    _this.find('.progress_comment_img').hide();
                }
            }
        });
    }

	function slider_sidebar()
    {
        $('.sidebar').not('.sidebar--hidden').find('.slider--sidebar').not('.slider_slick_initied').each(function() {
            $(this).addClass('slider_slick_initied');
            var slides_num = 3; // по-умолчанию 3
			var real_slides_num = $(this).find('.inner--slider--sidebar, .inner--slider--sidebar1').length;
            if (!('showinlimbo' in window)) { // если включен adblock
                if(real_slides_num < 6) { // если меньше 6ти слайдов
                    slides_num = Math.min(3, real_slides_num);
                } else { // если больше 6ти слайдов
                    slides_num = 6;
                }
            } else { // если выключен adblock
                slides_num = Math.min(3, real_slides_num);;
            }

            if($(this).parents('.sidebar--video').length) { // если это видео, 4 кадра
                slides_num = 4;
            }

            $(this).slick({
                'vertical': true,
                'slidesToShow': slides_num,
                'slidesToScroll': slides_num,
                'prevArrow': '<button class="slider__arrow slider__arrow--up"></button>',
                'nextArrow': '<button class="slider__arrow slider__arrow--down"></button>',
            }).parent().addClass('items_'+slides_num);
            $('.sidebar__link', $(this)).each(function() {
                var boxHeight = $(this).innerHeight();
                var innerHeight = $('span',$(this)).innerHeight();
                if (innerHeight > boxHeight) {
                    $(this).addClass('ellipsis');
                }
            })
        });

        $('.sidebar').not('.sidebar--hidden').find('.best_dem .sidebar__img img').one("load", function() {
            $(this).parents('a').addClass('black_back');
        }).each(function() {
            // if(this.complete) $(this).load();
        });

        $(".slider--sidebar.comment--sidebar").simplyScroll({
            customClass : 'slider--sidebar-wrap',
            orientation : 'vertical',
            auto        : false,
            manualMode  : 'end',
            frameRate   : 60,
            speed       : 10,
            startOnLoad : true,
            callback    : function() {
                $('.comments_slider_overlay').css('visibility', 'visible');
                $('.comments_slider_overlay .simply-scroll-container:not(:first)').hide();
            }
        });
    }
	return {
		init: slider_init,
		sidebar: slider_sidebar
	};
})();

fishki.tpl = (function() {

	function author_arrow()
	{
		if($('.author--profile').length && $('.post').length) {
			var tags_top = Math.floor($('.content__tags').offset().top-$('.post').offset().top);
			$('.author--profile .arrow').css('top', (tags_top-1) + 'px');
			$('.author__status').css('min-height', Math.max(1,tags_top-176));
			$('.author--profile').css('min-height', Math.max(220,tags_top+44));
		}
	}

	return {
		author_arrow: author_arrow
	};

if (!fishki.redirect) fishki.redirect = {};

fishki.redirect = (function(from_full_version, domain, redirect_url){
	var version = {
		mobile: 'mobile',
		main: 'main'
	};

	function check_cookie_enable()
	{
			if (typeof $.cookie('e') == 'undefined')
				$.cookie('e', 1, {path: '/', domain: domain, expires: 365});
			return typeof $.cookie('e') != 'undefined';
	}

	function set_cookie_version(version)
	{
		$.cookie('_vs', version, {path: '/', domain: domain});
		$.cookie('_vse', 1, {path: '/', domain: domain, expires: 1});
	}

	function get_cookie_version()
	{
		return $.cookie('_vs') && $.cookie('_vse') ? $.cookie('_vs') : false;
	}

	function hide_mobile_warn()
	{
		$.cookie('_vs_warn', screen.width, { expires: 31 });
		$('.mobile-notify').hide();
		return false;
	}

	function hide_full_warn()
	{
		$.cookie('_vs_warn_m', screen.width, { expires: 7 });
		$('.full-notify').hide();
		return false;
	}

	function check_mobile_screen()
	{
		return (screen.width <= 640) || navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone/i) || (navigator.userAgent.match(/Tizen/i) && navigator.userAgent.match(/Mobile/i)) || ((navigator.userAgent.search(/Android/)!=-1) && (window.innerWidth*window.innerHeight <= 640*480));
	}

	function check_wide_screen()
	{
		return (screen.width >= 1024) && !navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone/i);
	}

	function warn(){
		if (from_full_version)
		{
			if (!$.cookie('_vs_warn') && check_mobile_screen())
			{
				document.write('<div class="top-notify mobile-notify form" style="width:100%; box-sizing: border-box">'+
					'<a href="#" onClick="fishki.redirect.hide_mobile_warn();" class="close">'+
						'<i class="ficon-cancel"></i>'+
					'</a>Вы просматриваете страницу с низким разрешением экрана. '+
					'<a class="btn btn-blue" onclick="fishki.redirect.set_cookie_version(fishki.redirect.version.mobile)" href="'+redirect_url+'">Перейти на мобильную версию</a> '+
					'<span class="b-green"></span>'+
				'</div>');

				$(window).bind('resize', function(){
					$('.top-notify').css({width: (((navigator.userAgent.search(/Android/)!=-1) ? window.innerWidth : Math.min(screen.width, $('#container>.wrapper').width()))-40)+'px'});
				}).trigger('resize');
			}
		}
		else
		{
			if (!$.cookie('_vs_warn_m'))
			{
				document.write('<div class="top-notify full-notify form" style="width:100%; box-sizing: border-box">'+
					'<a href="#" onClick="fishki.redirect.hide_full_warn();" class="close">'+
						'<i class="ficon-cancel"></i>'+
					'</a>'+
					'<a onclick="fishki.redirect.set_cookie_version(fishki.redirect.version.main)" href="'+redirect_url+'">Перейти на полную версию</a> '+
				'</div>');

				$(window).bind('resize', function(){
					$('.top-notify').css({width: (((navigator.userAgent.search(/Android/)!=-1) ? window.innerWidth : Math.min(screen.width, $('#container>.wrapper').width()))-40)+'px'});
				}).trigger('resize');
			}
		}
	}

	// Если куки не поддерживаются - не делаем проверок и редиректов
	if (!check_cookie_enable())
		return;

	var cookie_version = get_cookie_version();
	var external_referer = false;
	// Если зашёл в первый раз - определяем куда надо редиректить и устанавливаем куку, на какую версию произошёл редирект
	var check_redirect_from_mobile = true; // !cookie_version || external_referer;

	if (1)
	{
		// console.log('from_full_version: ', from_full_version, 'cookie_version: ', cookie_version, 'check_mobile_screen()', check_mobile_screen(), 'check_wide_screen()', check_wide_screen());
		if (from_full_version)
		{
			// Определяем, нужно ли редиректить на мобильную
			if ((cookie_version != version.main) && check_mobile_screen())
			{
				set_cookie_version(version.mobile);
				window.location = redirect_url;
			}
//			else
//				set_cookie_version(version.main);
		}
		else
		{
			if (check_wide_screen())
			{
				set_cookie_version(version.main);
				window.location = redirect_url;
			}
//			else
//				set_cookie_version(version.mobile);
		}
	}

	return {
		version: version,
		set_cookie_version: set_cookie_version,
		get_cookie_version: get_cookie_version,
		hide_mobile_warn: hide_mobile_warn,
		hide_full_warn: hide_full_warn,
		warn: warn
	}
})(true, "fishki.net", "http://m.fishki.net/gif/");    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">

<script>
	fishki.scroll.header.init();

	// Позиция скролла при клике на элемент с анкором
	$(document).on('mouseover', '.header .nav__block__link', function(event)
	{
		event.preventDefault();
		var target = $(this).data('id');

		$(this).parent('.nav__block__links').children('.nav__block__link').removeClass('active');
		$(this).parent().parent().find('.nav__block__content').addClass('hidden');
		$(this).addClass('active');
		$(target).removeClass('hidden');
	});

	$(document).on('click', '.header-settings__link_to', function(event)
	{
		if ($(this).hasClass('flag'))
			return;

		event.preventDefault();
		var val = $(this).parent().hasClass('active');
		$('.header-settings__item').removeClass('active');
		if (!val)
			$(this).parent().addClass('active');
	});
</script>

<script>
    $(document).on('change', '.content__filter input[name=feed_time]', function(event) {
        window.location.href = '/gif/';
    });
    $(function(){
        if (typeof $('').glDatePicker != "undefined") {
            $('.restrict-date2').glDatePicker(
                {
                    dowOffset: 1,
                    showAlways: false,
                    cssName: 'default',
                    appendTo: '.content__filter .datepicker',
                                        selectableDateRange: [
                        {
                            from: new Date(2004, 1, 1),
                            to: new Date()
                        }
                    ],
                    onClick: function (target, cell, date, data) {
                        var year = date.getFullYear();
                        var day = ('0' + date.getDate()).slice(-2);
                        var month = ('0' + (date.getMonth() + 1)).slice(-2);
                        target.val(year + '-' + month + '-' + day);
                        var url = '/gif/' + 'dayposts/' + target.val();
                        document.location.href = url;
                        return false;
                    },
                    onShow: function(calendar) {},
                    onHide: function(calendar) {}
            });
            
            
                        $(document).on('click', '.content__filter-tip__row.change_data', function(event) { $('#gldp-4255060049').toggle(); return false; });
                        
        }
    });

</div><div class='clearfix'></div></div>        <script>
            (function() {

    var elements = document.getElementsByClassName('ellipsize');

    function ellipsize() {
        tm_start('1 $titles.each');
        var num_of_rows = 1, i, length = elements.length;
        var str_height = 0;
        var titles = new Array(length);
        for (i=0; i<length; i++)
        {
            var el = elements[i];
            titles[i] = el.getElementsByClassName('content__title')[0];
            if (!str_height)
            {
                var span = titles[i].getElementsByTagName('span')[0];
                str_height = parseInt(getComputedStyle(span).getPropertyValue('line-height'));
            }
            num = titles[i].offsetHeight == 0 ? 1 : Math.floor(titles[i].scrollHeight / str_height);
            if (num > num_of_rows)
                num_of_rows = num;
        }

        var height_coef = (num_of_rows < 1 || num_of_rows > 3) ? 3 : num_of_rows;
        tm_end('1 $titles.each');
        tm_start('2 $titles.each');
        for (i=0; i<length; i++)
        {
            var el = elements[i];
            var title = el.getElementsByClassName('content__title')[0];
            var a = title.getElementsByTagName('a')[0];
            var spans = a.getElementsByTagName('span');
            var title = spans[0].textContent;
            var num_of_photos;

            if (typeof spans[1] != 'undefined') {
                num_of_photos = spans[1].textContent;
            }
            var wordArray = title.split(' ');
            while(Math.floor(titles[i].scrollHeight / str_height) > height_coef) {
                if (wordArray.length == 0) {
                    break;
                }
                wordArray.pop();
                a.innerHTML = '<span>' + wordArray.join(' ') + '...' + '</span>' + ((num_of_photos !== undefined) ? '<span class="content__title_span">' + num_of_photos + '</span>' : '');
            }
            titles[i].style.height = height_coef * str_height + 'px';
        }
        tm_end('2 $titles.each');
    }
    function setWidthPicture() {
        var previous_size = null;
        var is_equal_sizes = false, i, imgs = [];
        for (i=0; i < elements.length; i++)
        {
            var pic_holder = elements[i].getElementsByClassName('picture-holder')[0];
            if (pic_holder) {
                var image = pic_holder.getElementsByTagName('img')[0];
                imgs.push(image);
                if (image.naturalWidth !== undefined && image.naturalHeight !== undefined) {
                    var width  = image.naturalWidth;
                    var height = image.naturalHeight;
                    if (!previous_size) {
                        previous_size = {width: width, height: height};
                    }
                    else {
                        if (previous_size.width == width && previous_size.height == height) {
                            is_equal_sizes = true;
                        }
                        else {
                            is_equal_sizes = false;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        for (i=0; i < imgs.length; i++)
        {
            var image = imgs[i];
            if (is_equal_sizes)
                image.style.minHeight = '0px';
            else if (image.naturalWidth !== undefined && image.naturalHeight !== undefined) {
                    image.style.width = parseInt(image.naturalWidth * image.height / image.naturalHeight)+'px';
            }
        }
    }
    tm_start('ellipsize');
    ellipsize();
    tm_end('ellipsize');
    tm_start('setWidthPicture');
    setWidthPicture();
    tm_end('setWidthPicture');
}) ();        </script>

	var fbfeedPostMessage = function(){}, fbfeedPostMessage = function(){}, fbIsFan = function(callbackSUCCESS){callbackSUCCESS();};
	if (typeof FB !== 'undefined') {
		FB.XFBML.parse();
	} else {
		$.getScript('https://connect.facebook.net/ru_RU/sdk.js', function(){
			FB.init({
				appId: "205618126277069",
	//			status     : true, // check login status
	//			cookie     : true, // enable cookies to allow the server to access the session
	//			xfbml      : true,  // parse XFBML
				version    : "v2.4"
			});
			FB.Event.subscribe('edge.create', function(url, html_element){
				if ($(html_element).data('social'))
					$.post('/counter/share/', {data: $(html_element).data('social')});
					$(window).trigger('social.fb_subscribe');
			});
			FB.Event.subscribe('edge.remove', function(url, html_element){
				if ($(html_element).data('social'))
					$.post('/counter/share/', {data: $(html_element).data('social')+':dislike'});
					$(window).trigger('social.fb_unsubscribe');
			});

			// Reinit functions
			fbfeedPostMessage = function (post)
			{
				FB.getLoginStatus(function(response){

					if (response.status === 'connected')
					{
						FB.api('/me/permissions', function (response) {
							if(typeof(response.data) !='undefined')
							{
								FB.api('/me/feed', 'post', {message: post.message, link: post.link}, function(response) {});
							}
							else
							{
								FB.login(function(response) {
									if (response.authResponse) {
										FB.api('/me/feed', 'post', {message: post.message, link: post.link}, function(response) {});
									}
								}, {scope: "email,public_profile,publish_actions"});
								return false;
							}
						} );
					}
					else
					{
						FB.login(function(response) {
							if (response.authResponse) {
								FB.api('/me/feed', 'post', {message: post.message, link: post.link}, function(response) {});
							}
						}, {scope: "email,public_profile,publish_actions"});
					}
				});
			};

			fbIsFan = function(callbackSUCCESS, callbackFAILURE)
			{
				FB.getLoginStatus(function(response){
					if (response.authResponse) {
						var pageId = "109588389068542";
						var userId = response.authResponse.userID;
						FB.api('/' + pageId + '/members/' + userId, function(response) {
							if (response && response.data && response.data.length > 0)
								callbackSUCCESS();
							else if (typeof(callbackFAILURE) == 'function')
								callbackFAILURE();
						});
					}
				});
			};

			showFbDialog = function (feed_tag)
			{
				$feed = $(feed_tag);
				if (typeof FB != 'undefined')
				FB.ui(
					{
						method: 'feed',
						link: $feed.data('url'),
						display: 'popup'
					},
					function() {}
				);
				return false;
			};

			FB.XFBML.parse();
		});
	}
	var vkfeedPostMessage = function(){};
	if (typeof VK !== 'undefined') {
		$('.js-vk-like-button').each(function(index, value) {
			if ($(this).find('iframe').length < 1) {
				var pageId = null;
				var pageUrl = $(this).data('url') || null;
				var pageTitle = $(this).data('title') || $("meta[property='og:title']").attr('content').replace(/"+/g,"");
				var pageDescription = $(this).data('description') || $("meta[name=description]").attr('content').replace(/"+/g,"");
				var pageImage = $(this).data('image') || null;
				var buttonType = $(this).data('type') || 'button';
				var buttonHeight = $(this).data('height') || 22;
				var buttonWidth = $(this).data('width') || 150;

				var widgetId = VK.Widgets.Like($(this).attr('id'), {
					type : buttonType,
					height : buttonHeight,
					width : buttonWidth,
					pageUrl : pageUrl,
					pageTitle : pageTitle,
					pageDescription : pageDescription,
					pageImage : pageImage
				}, pageId);

				$(this).addClass('js-vk-widget-' + widgetId);
			}
		});
	} else {
		$.getScript('https://vk.com/js/api/openapi.js', function() {
			VK.init({apiId: "2758888", onlyWidgets: true});
			$('.js-vk-groups').each(function(index, value) {
				VK.Widgets.Group($(this).attr('id'), {mode: 1, width: "220", height: "140", color1: 'FFFFFF', color2: '2B587A', color3: '5B7FA6'}, 55774526);
			});
			$('.js-vk-like-button').each(function(index, value) {
				var pageId = null;
				var pageUrl = $(this).data('url') || null;
				var pageTitle = $(this).data('title') || $("meta[property='og:title']").attr('content').replace(/"+/g,"");
				var pageDescription = $(this).data('description') || $("meta[name=description]").attr('content').replace(/"+/g,"");
				var pageImage = $(this).data('image') || null;
				var buttonType = $(this).data('type') || 'button';
				var buttonHeight = $(this).data('height') || 22;
				var buttonWidth = $(this).data('width') || 150;

				var widgetId = VK.Widgets.Like($(this).attr('id'), {
					type : buttonType,
					height : buttonHeight,
					width : buttonWidth,
					pageUrl : pageUrl,
					pageTitle : pageTitle,
					pageDescription : pageDescription,
					pageImage : pageImage
				}, pageId);

				$(this).addClass('js-vk-widget-' + widgetId);
			});
			VK.Observer.subscribe("widgets.like.liked", function(likesCount, widgetId) {
				if (!widgetId)
					return;
				var $el = $('.js-vk-widget-'+widgetId);
				if ($el.length > 0)
					$.post('/counter/share/', {data: $el.data('social')});
			});
			VK.Observer.subscribe("widgets.like.unliked", function(likesCount, widgetId) {
				if (!widgetId)
					return;
				var $el = $('.js-vk-widget-'+widgetId);
				if ($el.length > 0)
					$.post('/counter/share/', {data: $el.data('social')+":dislike"});
			});

			// Reinit function
			vkfeedPostMessage = function(post)
			{
				VK.Auth.getLoginStatus(function(response) {
					if (response.session) {
						VK.Api.call(
							'wall.post',
							{
								'message': post.message,
								'attachments': post.link
							},
							function() {}
						);
					} else {
						VK.Auth.login(function(response) {
							if (response.session) {
								VK.Api.call(
									'wall.post',
									{
										'message': post.message,
										'attachments': post.link
									},
									function() {}
								);
							}
						},
							VK.access.FRIENDS
						);
					}
				});
			};
		});
	}

		if ($('#umode_switcher').hasClass('switcher_in_work'))
			return;
		var _this = $(this);
		$('#umode_switcher').addClass('switcher_in_work');
		$('#umode_switcher .sidebar__drop__selected').html(_this.html());
		$.post(
			'/user/usersTopMode/?users_mode=' + _this.data('umode')
		);
		$('.author__selector:visible').slideToggle(450);
		$('#userstop_' + _this.data('umode')).slideToggle(500, function() {
			$('#umode_switcher').removeClass('switcher_in_work');
		});
	});
</script>

	fishki.adv.refreshFloat = function()
	{
		var places = ['fishki_float_one_', 'fishki_float_two_'];
		var index, place_prefix;
		// Load
		for (index in places){
			place_prefix = places[index];
			for (i=1; i < rotated_size; i++)
			{
				$place = $('#'+place_prefix+i);
				if (!$place.html())
					$place.hide().html(adv_list[i-1][index]);
			}
		}
		// Fade out current
		for (index in places){
			place_prefix = places[index];
			$('#'+place_prefix+loaded_num).fadeOut('slow');
		}
		// Toggle index
		loaded_num++;
		if (loaded_num >= rotated_size)
			loaded_num = 0;
		// Fade in new place
		for (index in places){
			place_prefix = places[index];
			$('#'+place_prefix+loaded_num).fadeIn('slow');
		}
	};
}) ();

    (function(){
        $(window).on('resize.brand_ear', function(){
            var $main_section = $('.main-container'), $slider_top = $('.container-slider-top'), $adland = $('#medialand_adland_inline_div_2889, #medialand_adland_inline_div_2871, #fishki-branding'), top, href, w;
            if ($main_section.length && $adland && $adland.height() > 0)
            {
                top = $slider_top && $slider_top.length ? $slider_top.offset().top : $main_section.top;
                w = Math.floor($main_section.offset().left)+'px';
                href = $adland.find('a').attr('href');
                $('#brand-left-ear').width(w);
                $('#brand-right-ear').width(w);
                $('.brand-ear').css({top: top+'px'}).attr('href', href).attr('target', '_blank');
            }
        });
        $(window).trigger('resize.brand_ear');
    })();
</script>
